function [Weights] = BorderWeight_Irregular(T,im,Z,method)
2
% Usage: [Weights] = BorderWeight_Irregular(T,im,Z,method)
3
% Estimates the weights of an image based on the specific weighting model
4
%
as described in the report
5
%
6
%
7
% Inputs:
8
%
T:
The T constant(depends on the method)
9
%
im:
The input image(not used anymore)
10
%
Z:
The heights(where NaN is allowed to indicate edges)
11
%
method:
The weighting model, either s-shape or exponential
12
%
13
% Outputs:
14
%
Weights:
The assigned weights
15
%
16
%
17
%
18
% Last modified 02-06-2022
19
% Author: Martin Rossau , s164058
20
21
imnan = isnan(Z); % Find edges, edges/not part of the image = 1
22
23
imnan = padarray(imnan ,[1 1],1,'both'); % Add extra edges
24
25
dist = bwdist(imnan); % Find distance to edges
26
if strcmp(method ,'s-shape')
27
Weights = single(6*(dist./T).^5-15*(dist./T).^4+10*(dist./T).^3); % Add
weights
28
Weights(dist./T>=1) = 1; % Limit to 1, when above or at T
170
Optical Surface Navigation on Planetary Bodies
==PAGE:187==
Appendix E. Code
29
Weights(dist./T<=0) = 0; % Limit to 0, when below or at 0
30
elseif strcmp(method, 'exp')
31
Weights = single(1-exp(-dist./T)); % Add weights
32
end
33
Weights = Weights(2:end-1,2:end-1); % Remove added edges
34
35
end

Code/Stereo/ReferenceMapping.m
triangulateMap
1
function [wP,error] = triangulateMap(im1,im2,stereoParams ,gauss,errorThreshold
)
2
% Usage: [wP,error] = triangulateMap(im1,im2,stereoParams ,gauss,errorThreshold
)
3
% Finds matches between the two images and triangulates
4
%
5
%
6
% Inputs:
7
%
im1:
Left image
8
%
im2:
Right image
9
%
stereoParms:
Calibration of the stereo camera setup, made in
10
%
MATLAB stereo calibration tool
11
%
gauss:
The sigma for the gauss smoothing , if 0, then this
12
%
is disabled
13
%
errorThreshold:
The threshold of maximum allowed reprojection error
14
%
of the world points
15
%
16
%
17
% Outputs:
18
%
wP:
The triangulated points(3D)
19
%
error:
The reprojection erros of the triangulated world
20
%
points
21
%
22
% Last modified 01-06-2023
23
% Author: Martin Rossau , s164058
24
25
%% Convert to gray-scale images , as the features is only based on gray scale
26
im1x = rgb2gray(im1);
27
im2x = rgb2gray(im2);
28
%% Smoothing of the images if wanted
29
if gauss >0
30
im1x = imgaussfilt(im1x,gauss);
31
im2x = imgaussfilt(im2x,gauss);
32
end
33
%% Undistort images
34
im1x = undistortImage(im1x,stereoParams.CameraParameters1);
35
im2x = undistortImage(im2x,stereoParams.CameraParameters2);
36
37
38
%% Select the specific features to track
39
40
Points1 = detectSURFFeatures(im1x,'MetricThreshold',700);
41
Points2 = detectSURFFeatures(im2x,'MetricThreshold',700);
42
43
Points1 = detectSURFFeatures(im1x,'MetricThreshold',1500);
44
Points2 = detectSURFFeatures(im2x,'MetricThreshold',1500);
45
46
%% Ignore those that naturally would match, since they can't be seen in both
views
47
Points1 = Points1(Points1.Location(:,1) >1200);
48
Points2 = Points2(Points2.Location(:,1)<(size(im1,2) -1200));
49
50
%% Extract the features
51
[Features1 ,ValidPoints1] = extractFeatures(im1x,Points1);
52
[Features2 ,ValidPoints2] = extractFeatures(im2x,Points2);
178
Optical Surface Navigation on Planetary Bodies
==PAGE:195==
Appendix E. Code
53
54
%% Match the features
55
[indexPairs ,match] = matchFeatures(Features1 ,Features2 ,'Unique',false);
56
57
%[matchSorted ,matchOrder] = sort(match);
58
%% Sort by match strength
59
[~,matchOrder] = sort(match);
60
61
IndexPairs1 = indexPairs(matchOrder ,1);
62
IndexPairs2 = indexPairs(matchOrder ,2);
63
64
MatchedPoints1 = ValidPoints1(IndexPairs1 ,:);
65
MatchedPoints2 = ValidPoints2(IndexPairs2 ,:);
66
%% Do an initial RANSAC/MSAC if there is over 15 matches , to reduce the
outliers
67
if MatchedPoints1.Count >=15
68
[~,inliers] = estimateFundamentalMatrix(MatchedPoints1 ,MatchedPoints2 ,'
Method','MSAC','DistanceThreshold',1e0,'NumTrials',1000000);
69
MatchedPoints1(~inliers) = [];
70
MatchedPoints2(~inliers) = [];
71
end
72
73
%% Triangulate the matched features and remove those who have reprojection
error higher than the threshold
74
[worldPoints ,error,valid] = triangulate(MatchedPoints1 ,MatchedPoints2 ,
stereoParams);
75
Indices = error<errorThreshold;
76
wP = worldPoints(Indices ,:);
77
error = error(Indices ,:);
78
wP(:,2) = wP(:,2);
79
end
